NOTICE

2337

NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE.
V. Kodiyarasi, a female child born to P. Veerappa Govunder on 17-02-1989 residing at No. 8, Muththoppu Street,
Villupuram, has been living as a male after an elaborate F to M transsexual conversion surgery by Dr. Krishna G. Seshadri
Head Department of Endocrinology Diabetes and Metabolism Professor of Medicine and Endocrinology Sri Ramachandra
Medical College and Research Institute (Deemed University) Porur, Chennai, By this I, may be treated as a male and shall
henceforth be known as V. JAI.
V. KODIYARASI.
Villupuram,
